commit 2bfc16d4b6ee819f755a03a6cf97b90644a81835
Author: muupan <muupan@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 5 19:12:19 2018 +0900

    Explain why y is clipped
    
    I found clipping was necessary for training CategoricalDQN from earlier
    experiments. Without clipping, some probability values converges to 0,
    resulting in log(0) -> NaN.
    
    Other unofficial implementations also apply clipping.
    https://github.com/Kaixhin/Rainbow/blob/master/agent.py#L85
    https://github.com/floringogianu/categorical-dqn/blob/master/policy_improvement/categorical_update.py#L53
    
    Since clipping by 1e-10 worked, I didn't tune 1e-10 further. It is
    possible larger values may result in better performance.

    Define common interfaces for replay buffers
    
    The behaviour of episodic replay buffers has been changed so that now
    __len__ returns the number of transitions, not episodes, to fix
    https://github.com/chainer/chainerrl/issues/138. You can use the n_episodes
    property to get the number of episodes in the buffer.

commit 5c9cb731fc4ba002e56297d7543de11d503094f0
Author: muupan <muupan@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Jan 30 21:18:51 2017 +0900

    Use funcsigs.signature instead of inspect.getargspec
    
    In py2 inspect.getargspec doesn't support non-function callables and
    inspect.getargspec is deprecated. In py3 inspect.signature is
    recommended as an alternative to it, but it is not available in py2.
    funcsigs is a backport of inspect.signature.
